 The charge sheet accused Advani and other Sangh Parivar leaders of conspiring to demolish the disputed structure
 isi bich farvari 2001 main elahabaad hoicourt kii lakhanu bench ne exiaar number 198 ko raibareli se lakhanu transfar kiye jane ko takneekee taur par galat kaha kyonki iske liye rajya sarkaar ne hoicourt ke mukhya nyaayadhish se anumati nahin lee thi
 However, the High Court did not comment on the removal of the criminal conspiracy clause
 upi sarkaar ne takneekee galati durast nahin kii or exiaar number 198 kaa maamla waapas raibareli court chalaa gaya
 On May 4, 2001, Special Judge Srikant Shukla of the CBI Court of Lucknow dropped the criminal conspiracy against Advani and 20 other leaders because FIR 197 was only about the demolition of Babri Masjid and not criminal conspiracy
 baad main may 2010 main elahabaad hoicourt ne bhi is faisle ko barkaraar rakhaa
 Nine months after this decision, the CBI filed an application in the Supreme Court in February 2011
 adwani or baaki netaa yachika daayar main hui deree kaa aadhaar maanakar yachika khaarij kiye jane kii maang kar rahe the lekin court ne ye maang khaarij kar di
 Apart from the CBI, a petitioner, Haji Mahboob, had also filed an application in the Supreme Court that after changing the government at the Center in 2014, the CBI can change its stand
 bijepi or sangh se jude aropiyon ke khilaaf aapraadhik sajeesh ke tahat mukadmaa chalaaya janaa chahie
 Now the hearing on the petition of CBI and Haji Mehboob is complete and soon the Supreme Court will give its verdict in this case
 kings ilevan punjab ne dilli dairedevills ko 10 wicket se karaari shikast di
 He scored a modest target of 68 runs with 73 balls to spare
 hashim amala or martin gaptil ne 7
 68 runs without loss in 5 overs
 gaptil 50 or amala 16 ran banaakar naabad laute
 Mumbai has the record of winning the most balls remaining
 usne 2008 main 87 genden rahete keker ko 8 wicket se maat di thi
 In 2011, the Kochi Tuskers defeated Rajasthan Royals with 76 balls remaining
 is lihaaj se punjab kii yah teesri badi jeet he
 Kings XI Punjab won the IPL by 10 wickets for the first time
 punjab ne 9 maichon main chaar jeet ke saath apni plaop kii ummiden jinda rakhi hai
 While Delhi has got the sixth defeat in 8 matches
 dilli kii shuruyaat bigaadane vaale sandip sharma main of da match rahe
 Delhi reduced their lowest score to 67, without captain Zaheer Khan bowling Delhi Daredevils for 67 runs by Kings XI Punjab
 jahir kii gairmaujuudagi main karun nair ko captaini raas nahin ai
 This is Delhi's lowest score in the IPL
 ipel main 49 (RCB) or 58 (RR) ran ke baad overol teesraa sabase kam score he
 KKR also has a minimum score of 67
 dilli kii pari main teen ballebaaj hi dohare ank ko chhu paae
 Sandeep Sharma took 4 wickets for 20 runs in 4 overs
 jabaki akshar patel ne 4 over main 22 ran dekar do wicket nikaale
 Finally, Varun Aaron took 2 wickets for 3 runs in 2 overs
 dilli ke aakhri paanch wicket 37 ran par gire67 ke score par mo

 isi score par dilli ko aakhri jhatka laga

 Delhi's sixth wicket fell for 33 runs

 Captain Glenn Maxwell gave Delhi the fifth blow for 30 runs
 viketon ke patjhad ke bich karun nair (11 ran) ko akshar patel ne bold kar diya
 Delhi's fourth wicket fell at 25 runs
 dilli dairedevills kii ore se sanju samson or sam billings ne pari kii shuruyaat kii
 But Billings (0) wicket fell in the very first over
 sandip sharma ne unhen wicket ke peeche riddhimaan saaha ke haathon kaich karaayaa

 aakhirkaar samson ne tisare over kii teesri gend par match kaa pehla chaukaa lagaaya

 sandip sharma ne doosraa jhatka diya

 22 ke score par teesraa wicket gira
 Kings Punjab won the toss, bowling at the IS Bindra Stadium in LPCA Mohali, Kings XI Punjab won the toss and decided to bowl
 ipel-10 ke 36wein match main kings ilevan punjab or dilli dairedevills aamane-saamne hue

 is sijan ke 15wein match main dilli ne apane gharelu maidan par punjab ko 51 ranon se haraaya tha

 In a book written on the Congress, former Prime Minister Indira Gandhi has been blamed for damaging the party's electoral base in the Hindi-speaking regions, especially Uttar Pradesh
 pustak ‘e centinary history of di indian neshnal congress’ shrinkhalaa ke paanchaven ank main likhaa gaya he ki indira gandhi ne jamini str tak jane kii koshish to kii lekin apane kareebi sahyogiyon kii madad se party ke dhaanche main parivartan sheersh str se kiya, jiskaa niyantran kam logon ke paas rahaa
 This led to the collapse of the original organizational form of the Congress which was the basis of the party's strength in some states
 pustak ke mutabik, ‘‘1980 ke dashak ke madhya tak sanghathan ko or party ke chunavi aadhaar ko kaaphi nuksaan ho chukaa tha jisase ab tak yah ubar nahin saki he
 His efforts to control the party brought an end to internal democracy which led to the collapse of party branches in major states like Uttar Pradesh
 ’’gauratlab he ki party ke 125 saal puure hone ke maukey par varisht netaa pranav mukherjee kii adhyakshata main sampadakon ke ek samooh ne is pustak ko taiyaar kiya he jisamen congress ko prabhavit karne vaale anek muddon kaa bakhaan or vishleshan kiya gaya he
 In the preface to the book, Mukherjee has said that Congress wanted the experts to edit this issue and contribute to it so that an objective and scholarly view on the period being reviewed is not necessary and that party Have a view of pranav mukherjee ne likhaa he ki pustak main lekhakon dwaara vyakt vichaar congress party ke najariye ko nahin jhalkaate
 It is not the official Congress history of the period between 1964 and 1984

 In the book, Sudha Pai writes in an article examining the political and social scenario in the six elections held during the said period, "at a time when the situation in the country and in the party (indira) is to achieve Gandhi's vision of change
" Mature, she moved into personal-centered politics which resulted in centralization of power in her hands
 ’’ lekh ke anusaar indira ne aam sahmati vaale netritv ke bajaay vyaktigat soch vaali raajnneeti ko apanaaya

" ’’pustak main likhaa he, ‘‘(indira) gandhi ko deshbhar ke rajyon main tamaam sakasham netaaon ke saath ek bhaleebhanti sangathit party viraasat main mili thi
 But neglecting the party machinery, he demoted a party dominance and started the process of long-term decay of the party organization, especially in North India
 ’’ lekhakon kaa vichaar he ki in ghatnakramon kaa tatkaal prabhaav mahasoos nahin kiya gaya or 1990 ke dashak main party ko nuksaan hota dekha gaya

 pustak ke anusaar, ‘‘kendrikaran kaa ahm parinaam pradeshon main congress party mashinari ke kshay or vighatan ke taur par hua

 pustak main likhaa gaya he, ‘‘uttar pradesh, jo congress ke liye mahatvapurn pradesh tha, main 1977 ke baad party kii 800 sahakaari samitiyon main koi chunaav nahin hua jo ki sthaneey vidhansabhaon se mahatvapurn tareeke se sambandhit thim
 "according to this," the party hardly had national and state-level leaders with independent bases of political power until the mid-1970s compared to the 1950s and 1960s

 com / utoxxsd8o5— ANI (@ani)september 8, 2019is maamle main fanse hai congress netabta den ki mani londring nirodhak kanoon (PMLA) ke tahat pravartan nideshaalay (ED) ne congress netaa dike sivakumar ko 3 sitambar ko giraftaar kiya tha
 DK Shivakumar was on the income tax and ED radar since the 2016 demonetisation
 2 agast 2017 ko unke nai dilli awaas par inakam tex ne chapa maaraa tha, jisamen 8
 Rs 59 crore cash was seized
 iske baad iskar vibhaag ne congress netaa or unke chaar anya sahyogiyon ke khilaaf maamla darj kiya
 Based on the charge sheet of the Income Department, the ED had lodged a case of money laundering against Shivkumar
 is maamle main giraftaar congress netaa dike sivakumar kii jamaanat arji dilli ke rouj avenue court ne pichley dinon khaarij kar diya tha
 After this, the court has sent him to ed's custody till 13 September
 varun gandhi dwaara baagi tevar dikhaae jane ke baad buudhvaar shaam tak yah khabar bhi ai ki unka naam star prachaarkon kii suchi se bijepi ne hataa diya he lekin isse pehle hi bijepi dwaara pichley hafte chunaav ayog ko chathe or saatven charan ke star prachaarkon kii jo suchi bheji gai thi, usase unka naam hataa diya gaya tha
 The rebellious attitude of Varun came to see after that
 unki jagah kendriya mantri manoj sinha kaa naam shaamil kiya gaya he
 It is worth mentioning that due to lack of attention in UP, BJP MP Varun Gandhi is looking very angry and his anger has come out in Indore
 indore ke ek kaarykram main varun ne system par jamkar hamalaa bolaa
 Varun also accused the system of failing in the development of minorities
 varun gandhi ne is kaarykram main rohit vemula ke suicide kaa mudda bhi uthaaya
 He said that he got crying after reading the suicide note of Rohit Vemula
 kisaanon kii aatmahatya ke mudde par bhi unhone kaha ki desh main karj vasuuli main bhedbhaav kiya ja rahaa he or amiron ko to riyaayat de di jaati he, lekin garib ko jaan deni padati he
 Varun said- In the last 2 years, the official data is that 7500 farmers committed suicide
 jabaki sachai main sankhya 50 hajaar ke aasapaas he
 Look at Vijay Mallya who had a loan of 10 thousand crores, he fled the country as soon as he got notice
 sawaal ek shaks kaa nahin, sawaal vyavastha kaa he
 With this, Varun said that it is a matter of shame that a Dalit phd student committed suicide in Hyderabad last year
 jab maine unki chitthee padhi mujhe ronaa aa gaya
 Rohit said in the letter that i am taking my life because i have committed the sin of being born in this form
 khaas baat yah he ki upi chunaav se pehle bijepi ke jin star prachaarkon kii list jari kii gai thi usamen varun gandhi kaa naam nahin tha haalanki baad main unka naam joda gaya tha
 Apart from this, he is also said to be angry with the party on the issue of ticket distribution of candidates in his constituency
 varun gandhi sultanpur se bijepi saansad hai jabaki unki maa or kendriya mantri menka gandhi pilibhit se saansad hai
 The comments ullekhneey he ki upi main tavajjo nahin milane se bijepi saansad varun gandhi khaase naaraaz dikhaai de rahe hai or unki yah bhadaas indore main jaakar nikali he
 At an event in Indore, Varun attacked the system fiercely
 varun ne system par alpsankhyakon ke vikaas main fail hone kaa aarope bhi lagaaya
 Varun Gandhi also raised the issue of Rohit Vemula's suicide at the event
 unhone kaha ki rohit vemula kaa suicide note padhakar unhen ronaa aa gaya
 On the issue of farmer suicides too, he said that there is discrimination in debt collection in the country and concessions are given to the rich, but the poor have to die
 varun ne kaha- pichley 2 saal main sarkari aankada he ki 7500 kisaanon ne aatmahatya kii
 While in reality the number is around 50 thousand
 vijay maalya ko dekhen jiske paas 10 hajaar karod kaa lone tha, jaise hi use notice gaya vah desh chhodkar bhaag gaya
 The question is not about one person but the question is of the system
 iske saath hi varun ne kaha ki bade shame kii baat he ki pichley saal hyderabad main ek dalit piechdi student ne aatmahatya kar lee
 When i read his letter, i started crying
 rohit ne chitthee main ye kaha ki main apni jaan isliye le rahaa hum kyonki maine is rup main janm lene kaa paap kiya he
 The special thing is that Varun Gandhi's name was not in the list of star campaigners of BJP which was released before the UP elections, although his name was added later
 iske alaava apane kshetra main ummidavaaron ke tikat bantwaare ke mudde par bhi vah party se naaraaz bataae ja rahe hai
